name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Boutique Room - City-View (2 beds)
info:Stayed in September 2023
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:3.5
posted:Posted September 16, 2023
msg:I came here more than 20 years ago, when the domestic tourism industry had not yet emerged. As an early five-star hotel, the Minshan Hotel was really not low-grade, and it was almost incomparable with other guest houses and hotels. It was far ahead.
However, now that high-end hotels are popping up everywhere, it is not appropriate to measure them by the standards of the past.
Of course, Minshan Hotel still has great advantages in terms of location, service, sanitation and other conditions, especially staff service, which is the most difficult item to perfect. Minshan Hotel deserves to be an old five-star hotel and can be praised.
But in terms of hardware facilities, which are the easiest to build, why are you lame at Minshan Hotel?
Putting aside the structural factors of the house that cannot be improved due to historical reasons, let‚Äôs briefly list a few:
1. Take a look at the attached picture 1. You can‚Äôt wash your face in the washbasin at all. The water faucet is long and high, and you can't lower your head. If you really dare to lower your head and close your eyes to splash water on your face as usual, you may be blinded by the faucet. So, I had to use a towel to soak up some water, wet it and wipe my face. Just like that, I still got water splashing all over the bathroom floor. It would be perfect if the hotel could provide a plastic washbasin in each room so that you can take a basin of water to wash your face.
2. Take a look at the attached picture 2. After the glass door of the bathing area is closed, there is a gap on the side and bottom of the door, which is quite wide. So after taking a bath, the bathroom floor is a mess, water is flowing all over the floor, and the foot towels are also completely wet. It‚Äôs really Worry about slipping and falling injuries will add trouble to the hotel. Combined with item 1 above, the bathroom floor has never been dry when people are in the guest room.
Why not refer to other hotels and use a push-pull glass door, which perfectly solves the problem of side and bottom seams, and also solves the problem that the opening and closing door takes up a lot of space and is easy to hit people. Use a horizontal handle and you can hang bath towels. What, never seen it? I'm attaching Figure 3 for reference.
3. So the simplest ones, things like body wash and shampoo are easy to make, right? Unfortunately, it didn't work out either. Take a look at the attached picture 4. All toiletries are carved from the same mold, with the same color and pattern. When your guests are drenched with water, are you still struggling to read the words written on this small plastic tube? I have presbyopia and I have to get wet and go out of the bathroom to get my glasses. Can't we just make a difference in color?
To sum up, I have to go against the ancestral precepts and give a sincere evaluation of this accommodation experience.
